<s> in addition president asad signed legislative decrees to encourage corporate ownership reform and to allow the central bank to issue treasury bills and bonds for government debt <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy remains highly controlled by the government <\s>
<s> long-run economic constraints include declining oil production high unemployment rising budget deficits and increasing pressure on water supplies caused by heavy use in agriculture rapid population growth industrial expansion and water pollution <\s>
<s> taiwan taiwan has a dynamic capitalist economy with gradually decreasing government guidance of investment and foreign trade <\s>
<s> in keeping with this trend some large state-owned banks and industrial firms have been privatized <\s>
<s> exports led by electronics and machinery generate about 70 of taiwan's gdp growth and have provided the primary impetus for economic development <\s>
<s> this heavy dependence on exports makes the economy vulnerable to downturns in world demand <\s>
<s> in 2009 taiwan's gdp fell by 1.9 due primarily to a 20 year-on-year decline in exports <\s>
<s> gdp grew more than 8 in 2010 as exports returned to the level of previous years <\s>
<s> taiwan's diplomatic isolation low birth rate and rapidly aging population are major long-term challenges <\s>
<s> free trade agreements have proliferated in east asia over the past several years but so far taiwan has been excluded from this greater economic integration largely for reasons of diplomacy <\s>
<s> taiwan's birth rate of only 1.2 child per woman is among the lowest in the world raising the prospect of future labor shortages falling domestic demand and declining tax revenues <\s>
<s> taiwan's population is aging quickly with the number of people over 65 accounting for 10.8 of the island's total population as of the end of 2009 <\s>
<s> the island runs a large trade surplus and its foreign reserves are the world's fourth largest behind china japan and russia <\s>
<s> since president ma ying-jeou took office in may 2008 cross-strait economic ties have increased significantly <\s>
<s> since 2005 china has overtaken the us to become taiwan's second-largest source of imports after japan <\s>
<s> china is also the island's number one destination for foreign direct investment <\s>
<s> taipei has focused much of its economic recovery effort on improving cross-strait economic integration <\s>
<s> three financial memorandums of understanding covering banking securities and insurance took effect in mid-january 2010 opening the island to greater investments from the mainland's financial firms and institutional investors and providing new opportunities for taiwan financial firms to operate in china <\s>
<s> taiwan and the mainland in june 2010 signed the landmark economic cooperation framework agreement ecfa an agreement similar to a free-trade agreement deal that will increase cross-strait economic ties by lowering tariffs on a number of goods <\s>
<s> taiwan's goverment has said that the ecfa will serve as a stepping stone toward trade pacts with other regional partners and announced the beginning of negotiations on such an agreement with singapore in august <\s>
<s> tajikistan tajikistan has one of the lowest per capita gdps among the 15 former soviet republics <\s>
<s> because of a lack of employment opportunities in tajikistan nearly half of the labor force works abroad primarily in russia and kazakhstan supporting families in tajikistan through remittances <\s>
<s> the exact number of labor migrants is unknown but estimated at around 1 million <\s>
<s> less than 7 of the land area is arable <\s>
<s> cotton is the most important crop but this sector is burdened with debt and obsolete infrastructure moreover government has encouraged a gradual transition away from cotton and towards food cultivation due to its concerns about feeding the population <\s>
<s> mineral resources include silver gold uranium and tungsten <\s>
<s> industry consists only of a large aluminum plant hydropower facilities and small obsolete factories mostly in light industry and food processing <\s>
<s> the civil war 1992-97 severely damaged the already weak economic infrastructure and caused a sharp decline in industrial and agricultural production <\s>
<s> tajikistan's economic situation remains fragile due to uneven implementation of structural reforms corruption weak governance seasonal power shortages and the external debt burden <\s>
<s> a debt restructuring agreement was reached with russia in december 2002 including a 250 million write-off of tajikistan's 300 million debt <\s>
<s> completion of the sangtuda i hydropower dam finished in 2009 with russian investment and the sangtuda ii and rogun dams will add substantially to electricity output <\s>
<s> if finished according to tajik plans rogun will be the world's tallest dam <\s>
<s> the world bank in 2010 agreed to fund safety and feasibility studies for the rogun dam <\s>
<s> favorable reports from these studies could increase investor interest in the project which has been stalled due to lack of funding <\s>
<s> tajikistan has also received substantial infrastructure development loans from the chinese government to improve roads and an electricity transmission network <\s>
<s> to help increase north-south trade the us funded a 36 million bridge which opened in august 2007 and links tajikistan and afghanistan <\s>
<s> while tajikistan has experienced steady economic growth since 1997 more than half of the population continues to live in poverty <\s>
<s> economic growth reached 10.6 in 2004 but dropped below 8 in 2005-08 as the effects of higher oil prices and then the international financial crisis began to register mainly in the form of lower prices for key export commodities and lower remittances from tajiks working abroad due to the global economic downturn <\s>
<s> in 2009 gdp growth dropped to 3.4 as a result of the world recession <\s>
<s> tanzania tanzania is one of the world's poorest economies in terms of per capita income however tanzania average 7 gdp growth per year between 2000 and 2008 on strong gold production and tourism <\s>
<s> the economy depends heavily on agriculture which accounts for more than one-fourth of gdp provides 85 of exports and employs about 60 of the work force <\s>
<s> the world bank the imf and bilateral donors have provided funds to rehabilitate tanzania's aging economic infrastructure including rail and port infrastructure that are important trade links for inland countries <\s>
<s> recent banking reforms have helped increase private-sector growth and investment and the government has increased spending on agriculture to 7 of its budget <\s>
<s> continued donor assistance and solid macroeconomic policies supported a positive growth rate despite the world recession <\s>
<s> in 2008 tanzania received the world's largest millennium challenge compact grant worth 698 million <\s>
<s> dar es salaam used fiscal stimulus and loosened monitary policy to ease the impact of the global recession <\s>
<s> gdp growth in 2009-10 was a respectable 6 per year due to high gold prices and increased production <\s>
<s> thailand with a well-developed infrastructure a free-enterprise economy generally pro-investment policies and strong export industries thailand enjoyed solid growth from 2000 to 2008 averaging more than 4 per year as it recovered from the asian financial crisis of 1997-98 <\s>
<s> thai exports mostly machinery and electronic components agricultural commodities and jewelry continue to drive the economy accounting for more than half of gdp <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis of 2008-09 severely cut thailand's exports with most sectors experiencing double-digit drops <\s>
<s> in 2009 the economy contracted 2.2 <\s>
<s> in 2010 thailand's economy expanded 7.6 its fastest pace since 1995 as exports rebounded from their depressed 2009 level <\s>
<s> antigovernment protests during march-may and the country's polarized political situation had at most a temporary impact on business and consumer confidence <\s>
<s> although tourism was hit hard during the protests its quick recovery helped boost consumer confidence to new highs <\s>
<s> moreover business and investor sentiment remained buoyant as thailand's stock market grew almost 5 during the three-month period <\s>
<s> the economy probably will continue to experience high grow well into 2011 <\s>
<s> timor-leste in late 1999 about 70 of the economic infrastructure of timor-leste was laid waste by indonesian troops and anti-independence militias <\s>
<s> three hundred thousand people fled westward <\s>
<s> over the next three years a massive international program manned by 5,000 peacekeepers (8 000 at peak and 1,300 police officers led to substantial reconstruction in both urban and rural areas <\s>
<s> by the end of 2005 refugees had returned or had settled in indonesia <\s>
<s> the country continues to face great challenges in rebuilding its infrastructure strengthening the civil administration and generating jobs for young people entering the work force <\s>
<s> the development of oil and gas resources in offshore waters has greatly supplemented government revenues <\s>
<s> this technology-intensive industry however has done little to create jobs for the unemployed because there are no production facilities in timor <\s>
<s> gas is piped to australia <\s>
<s> in june 2005 the national parliament unanimously approved the creation of a petroleum fund to serve as a repository for all petroleum revenues and to preserve the value of timor-leste's petroleum wealth for future generations <\s>
<s> the fund held assets of us 5.3 billion as of october 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy has been little impacted by the global financial crisis and continues to recover strongly from the mid 2006 outbreak of violence and civil unrest which disrupted both private and public sector economic activity <\s>
<s> the government in 2008 resettled tens of thousands of an estimated 100,000 internally displaced persons idps ); most idps returned home by early 2009 <\s>
<s> the underlying economic policy challenge the country faces remains how best to use oil-and-gas wealth to lift the non-oil economy onto a higher growth path and to reduce poverty <\s>
<s> togo this small sub-saharan economy suffers from anemic economic growth and depends heavily on both commercial and subsistence agriculture which provides employment for 65 of the labor force <\s>
<s> some basic foodstuffs must still be imported <\s>
<s> cocoa coffee and cotton generate about 40 of export earnings with cotton being the most important cash crop <\s>
<s> togo is the world's fourth-largest producer of phosphate <\s>
<s> the government's decade-long effort supported by the world bank and the imf to implement economic reform measures encourage foreign investment and bring revenues in line with expenditures has moved slowly <\s>
<s> progress depends on follow through on privatization increased openness in government financial operations progress toward legislative elections and continued support from foreign donors <\s>
<s> togo is on track with its imf extended credit facility and reached a hipc debt relief completion point in 2010 at which 95 of the country's debt was forgiven <\s>
<s> economic growth prospects remain marginal due to declining cotton production and underinvestment in phosphate mining <\s>
<s> tokelau tokelau's small size three villages isolation and lack of resources greatly restrain economic development and confine agriculture to the subsistence level <\s>
<s> the people rely heavily on aid from new zealand about 10 million annually in 2008 and 2009 to maintain public services <\s>
<s> new zealand's support amounts to 80 of tokelau's recurrent government budget <\s>
<s> an international trust fund currently worth nearly us 32 million was established in 2004 to provide tokelau an independent source of revenue <\s>
<s> the principal sources of revenue come from sales of copra postage stamps souvenir coins and handicrafts <\s>
<s> despite strong finances and underlying fundamentals the swedish economy slid into recession in the third quarter of 2008 and growth continued downward in 2009 as deteriorating global conditions reduced export demand and consumption <\s>
<s> strong exports of commodities and a return to profitability by sweden's banking sector drove the strong rebound in 2010 <\s>
<s> switzerland switzerland is a peaceful prosperous and modern market economy with low unemployment a highly skilled labor force and a per capita gdp among the highest in the world <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy benefits from a highly developed service sector led by financial services and a manufacturing industry that specializes in high-technology knowledge-based production <\s>
<s> the swiss have brought their economic practices largely into conformity with the eu's in order to enhance their international competitiveness but some trade protectionism remains particularly for its small agricultural sector <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis and resulting economic downturn put switzerland in a recession in 2009 as global export demand stalled <\s>
<s> the swiss national bank during this period effectively implemented a zero-interest rate policy in a bid to boost the economy and prevent appreciation of the franc <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy grew 2.8 in 2010 when bern implemented a third fiscal stimulus program but its prized banking sector has recently faced significant challenges <\s>
<s> the country's largest banks suffered sizable losses in 2008-09 leading its largest bank to accept a government rescue deal in late 2008 <\s>
<s> switzerland has also come under increasing pressure from individual neighboring countries the eu the us and international institutions to reform its banking secrecy laws <\s>
<s> consequently the government agreed to conform to oecd regulations on administrative assistance in tax matters including tax evasion <\s>
<s> the government has renegotiated its double taxation agreements with numerous countries including the us to incorporate the oecd standard and it is working with germany and the uk to resolve outsanding issues particularly the possibility of imposing taxes on bank deposits held by foreigners <\s>
<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>

<s> completion of the sangtuda i hydropower dam finished in 2009 with russian investment and the sangtuda ii and rogun dams will add substantially to electricity output <\s>
<s> if finished according to tajik plans rogun will be the world's tallest dam <\s>
<s> the world bank in 2010 agreed to fund safety and feasibility studies for the rogun dam <\s>
<s> favorable reports from these studies could increase investor interest in the project which has been stalled due to lack of funding <\s>
<s> tajikistan has also received substantial infrastructure development loans from the chinese government to improve roads and an electricity transmission network <\s>
<s> to help increase north-south trade the us funded a 36 million bridge which opened in august 2007 and links tajikistan and afghanistan <\s>
<s> while tajikistan has experienced steady economic growth since 1997 more than half of the population continues to live in poverty <\s>
<s> economic growth reached 10.6 in 2004 but dropped below 8 in 2005-08 as the effects of higher oil prices and then the international financial crisis began to register mainly in the form of lower prices for key export commodities and lower remittances from tajiks working abroad due to the global economic downturn <\s>
<s> in 2009 gdp growth dropped to 3.4 as a result of the world recession <\s>
<s> tanzania tanzania is one of the world's poorest economies in terms of per capita income however tanzania average 7 gdp growth per year between 2000 and 2008 on strong gold production and tourism <\s>
<s> the economy depends heavily on agriculture which accounts for more than one-fourth of gdp provides 85 of exports and employs about 60 of the work force <\s>
<s> the world bank the imf and bilateral donors have provided funds to rehabilitate tanzania's aging economic infrastructure including rail and port infrastructure that are important trade links for inland countries <\s>
<s> recent banking reforms have helped increase private-sector growth and investment and the government has increased spending on agriculture to 7 of its budget <\s>
<s> continued donor assistance and solid macroeconomic policies supported a positive growth rate despite the world recession <\s>
<s> in 2008 tanzania received the world's largest millennium challenge compact grant worth 698 million <\s>
<s> dar es salaam used fiscal stimulus and loosened monitary policy to ease the impact of the global recession <\s>
<s> gdp growth in 2009-10 was a respectable 6 per year due to high gold prices and increased production <\s>
<s> thailand with a well-developed infrastructure a free-enterprise economy generally pro-investment policies and strong export industries thailand enjoyed solid growth from 2000 to 2008 averaging more than 4 per year as it recovered from the asian financial crisis of 1997-98 <\s>
<s> thai exports mostly machinery and electronic components agricultural commodities and jewelry continue to drive the economy accounting for more than half of gdp <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis of 2008-09 severely cut thailand's exports with most sectors experiencing double-digit drops <\s>
<s> in 2009 the economy contracted 2.2 <\s>
<s> in 2010 thailand's economy expanded 7.6 its fastest pace since 1995 as exports rebounded from their depressed 2009 level <\s>
<s> antigovernment protests during march-may and the country's polarized political situation had at most a temporary impact on business and consumer confidence <\s>
<s> although tourism was hit hard during the protests its quick recovery helped boost consumer confidence to new highs <\s>
<s> moreover business and investor sentiment remained buoyant as thailand's stock market grew almost 5 during the three-month period <\s>
<s> the economy probably will continue to experience high grow well into 2011 <\s>
<s> timor-leste in late 1999 about 70 of the economic infrastructure of timor-leste was laid waste by indonesian troops and anti-independence militias <\s>
<s> three hundred thousand people fled westward <\s>
<s> over the next three years a massive international program manned by 5,000 peacekeepers (8 000 at peak and 1,300 police officers led to substantial reconstruction in both urban and rural areas <\s>
<s> by the end of 2005 refugees had returned or had settled in indonesia <\s>
<s> the country continues to face great challenges in rebuilding its infrastructure strengthening the civil administration and generating jobs for young people entering the work force <\s>
<s> the development of oil and gas resources in offshore waters has greatly supplemented government revenues <\s>
<s> this technology-intensive industry however has done little to create jobs for the unemployed because there are no production facilities in timor <\s>
<s> gas is piped to australia <\s>
<s> in june 2005 the national parliament unanimously approved the creation of a petroleum fund to serve as a repository for all petroleum revenues and to preserve the value of timor-leste's petroleum wealth for future generations <\s>
<s> the fund held assets of us 5.3 billion as of october 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy has been little impacted by the global financial crisis and continues to recover strongly from the mid 2006 outbreak of violence and civil unrest which disrupted both private and public sector economic activity <\s>
<s> the government in 2008 resettled tens of thousands of an estimated 100,000 internally displaced persons idps ); most idps returned home by early 2009 <\s>
<s> the underlying economic policy challenge the country faces remains how best to use oil-and-gas wealth to lift the non-oil economy onto a higher growth path and to reduce poverty <\s>
<s> togo this small sub-saharan economy suffers from anemic economic growth and depends heavily on both commercial and subsistence agriculture which provides employment for 65 of the labor force <\s>
<s> some basic foodstuffs must still be imported <\s>
<s> cocoa coffee and cotton generate about 40 of export earnings with cotton being the most important cash crop <\s>
<s> togo is the world's fourth-largest producer of phosphate <\s>
<s> the government's decade-long effort supported by the world bank and the imf to implement economic reform measures encourage foreign investment and bring revenues in line with expenditures has moved slowly <\s>
<s> progress depends on follow through on privatization increased openness in government financial operations progress toward legislative elections and continued support from foreign donors <\s>
<s> togo is on track with its imf extended credit facility and reached a hipc debt relief completion point in 2010 at which 95 of the country's debt was forgiven <\s>
<s> economic growth prospects remain marginal due to declining cotton production and underinvestment in phosphate mining <\s>
<s> tokelau tokelau's small size three villages isolation and lack of resources greatly restrain economic development and confine agriculture to the subsistence level <\s>
<s> the people rely heavily on aid from new zealand about 10 million annually in 2008 and 2009 to maintain public services <\s>
<s> new zealand's support amounts to 80 of tokelau's recurrent government budget <\s>
<s> an international trust fund currently worth nearly us 32 million was established in 2004 to provide tokelau an independent source of revenue <\s>
<s> the principal sources of revenue come from sales of copra postage stamps souvenir coins and handicrafts <\s>
<s> despite strong finances and underlying fundamentals the swedish economy slid into recession in the third quarter of 2008 and growth continued downward in 2009 as deteriorating global conditions reduced export demand and consumption <\s>
<s> strong exports of commodities and a return to profitability by sweden's banking sector drove the strong rebound in 2010 <\s>
<s> switzerland switzerland is a peaceful prosperous and modern market economy with low unemployment a highly skilled labor force and a per capita gdp among the highest in the world <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy benefits from a highly developed service sector led by financial services and a manufacturing industry that specializes in high-technology knowledge-based production <\s>
<s> the swiss have brought their economic practices largely into conformity with the eu's in order to enhance their international competitiveness but some trade protectionism remains particularly for its small agricultural sector <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis and resulting economic downturn put switzerland in a recession in 2009 as global export demand stalled <\s>
<s> the swiss national bank during this period effectively implemented a zero-interest rate policy in a bid to boost the economy and prevent appreciation of the franc <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy grew 2.8 in 2010 when bern implemented a third fiscal stimulus program but its prized banking sector has recently faced significant challenges <\s>
<s> the country's largest banks suffered sizable losses in 2008-09 leading its largest bank to accept a government rescue deal in late 2008 <\s>
<s> switzerland has also come under increasing pressure from individual neighboring countries the eu the us and international institutions to reform its banking secrecy laws <\s>
<s> consequently the government agreed to conform to oecd regulations on administrative assistance in tax matters including tax evasion <\s>
<s> the government has renegotiated its double taxation agreements with numerous countries including the us to incorporate the oecd standard and it is working with germany and the uk to resolve outsanding issues particularly the possibility of imposing taxes on bank deposits held by foreigners <\s>
<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>
<s> syria syrian economic growth slowed to 1.8 in 2009 as the global economic crisis affected oil prices and the economies of syria's key export partners and sources of investment <\s>
<s> damascus has implemented modest economic reforms in the past few years including cutting lending interest rates opening private banks consolidating all of the multiple exchange rates raising prices on some subsidized items most notably gasoline and cement and establishing the damascus stock exchange which began operations in 2009 <\s>
<s> in addition president asad signed legislative decrees to encourage corporate ownership reform and to allow the central bank to issue treasury bills and bonds for government debt <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy remains highly controlled by the government <\s>
<s> long-run economic constraints include declining oil production high unemployment rising budget deficits and increasing pressure on water supplies caused by heavy use in agriculture rapid population growth industrial expansion and water pollution <\s>
<s> taiwan taiwan has a dynamic capitalist economy with gradually decreasing government guidance of investment and foreign trade <\s>
<s> in keeping with this trend some large state-owned banks and industrial firms have been privatized <\s>
<s> exports led by electronics and machinery generate about 70 of taiwan's gdp growth and have provided the primary impetus for economic development <\s>
<s> this heavy dependence on exports makes the economy vulnerable to downturns in world demand <\s>
<s> in 2009 taiwan's gdp fell by 1.9 due primarily to a 20 year-on-year decline in exports <\s>
<s> gdp grew more than 8 in 2010 as exports returned to the level of previous years <\s>
<s> taiwan's diplomatic isolation low birth rate and rapidly aging population are major long-term challenges <\s>
<s> free trade agreements have proliferated in east asia over the past several years but so far taiwan has been excluded from this greater economic integration largely for reasons of diplomacy <\s>
<s> taiwan's birth rate of only 1.2 child per woman is among the lowest in the world raising the prospect of future labor shortages falling domestic demand and declining tax revenues <\s>
<s> taiwan's population is aging quickly with the number of people over 65 accounting for 10.8 of the island's total population as of the end of 2009 <\s>
<s> the island runs a large trade surplus and its foreign reserves are the world's fourth largest behind china japan and russia <\s>
<s> since president ma ying-jeou took office in may 2008 cross-strait economic ties have increased significantly <\s>
<s> since 2005 china has overtaken the us to become taiwan's second-largest source of imports after japan <\s>
<s> china is also the island's number one destination for foreign direct investment <\s>
<s> taipei has focused much of its economic recovery effort on improving cross-strait economic integration <\s>
<s> three financial memorandums of understanding covering banking securities and insurance took effect in mid-january 2010 opening the island to greater investments from the mainland's financial firms and institutional investors and providing new opportunities for taiwan financial firms to operate in china <\s>
<s> taiwan and the mainland in june 2010 signed the landmark economic cooperation framework agreement ecfa an agreement similar to a free-trade agreement deal that will increase cross-strait economic ties by lowering tariffs on a number of goods <\s>
<s> taiwan's goverment has said that the ecfa will serve as a stepping stone toward trade pacts with other regional partners and announced the beginning of negotiations on such an agreement with singapore in august <\s>
<s> tajikistan tajikistan has one of the lowest per capita gdps among the 15 former soviet republics <\s>
<s> because of a lack of employment opportunities in tajikistan nearly half of the labor force works abroad primarily in russia and kazakhstan supporting families in tajikistan through remittances <\s>
<s> the exact number of labor migrants is unknown but estimated at around 1 million <\s>
<s> less than 7 of the land area is arable <\s>
<s> cotton is the most important crop but this sector is burdened with debt and obsolete infrastructure moreover government has encouraged a gradual transition away from cotton and towards food cultivation due to its concerns about feeding the population <\s>
<s> mineral resources include silver gold uranium and tungsten <\s>
<s> industry consists only of a large aluminum plant hydropower facilities and small obsolete factories mostly in light industry and food processing <\s>
<s> the civil war 1992-97 severely damaged the already weak economic infrastructure and caused a sharp decline in industrial and agricultural production <\s>
<s> tajikistan's economic situation remains fragile due to uneven implementation of structural reforms corruption weak governance seasonal power shortages and the external debt burden <\s>
<s> a debt restructuring agreement was reached with russia in december 2002 including a 250 million write-off of tajikistan's 300 million debt <\s>

<s> this technology-intensive industry however has done little to create jobs for the unemployed because there are no production facilities in timor <\s>
<s> gas is piped to australia <\s>
<s> in june 2005 the national parliament unanimously approved the creation of a petroleum fund to serve as a repository for all petroleum revenues and to preserve the value of timor-leste's petroleum wealth for future generations <\s>
<s> the fund held assets of us 5.3 billion as of october 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy has been little impacted by the global financial crisis and continues to recover strongly from the mid 2006 outbreak of violence and civil unrest which disrupted both private and public sector economic activity <\s>
<s> the government in 2008 resettled tens of thousands of an estimated 100,000 internally displaced persons idps ); most idps returned home by early 2009 <\s>
<s> the underlying economic policy challenge the country faces remains how best to use oil-and-gas wealth to lift the non-oil economy onto a higher growth path and to reduce poverty <\s>
<s> togo this small sub-saharan economy suffers from anemic economic growth and depends heavily on both commercial and subsistence agriculture which provides employment for 65 of the labor force <\s>
<s> some basic foodstuffs must still be imported <\s>
<s> cocoa coffee and cotton generate about 40 of export earnings with cotton being the most important cash crop <\s>
<s> togo is the world's fourth-largest producer of phosphate <\s>
<s> the government's decade-long effort supported by the world bank and the imf to implement economic reform measures encourage foreign investment and bring revenues in line with expenditures has moved slowly <\s>
<s> progress depends on follow through on privatization increased openness in government financial operations progress toward legislative elections and continued support from foreign donors <\s>
<s> togo is on track with its imf extended credit facility and reached a hipc debt relief completion point in 2010 at which 95 of the country's debt was forgiven <\s>
<s> economic growth prospects remain marginal due to declining cotton production and underinvestment in phosphate mining <\s>
<s> tokelau tokelau's small size three villages isolation and lack of resources greatly restrain economic development and confine agriculture to the subsistence level <\s>
<s> the people rely heavily on aid from new zealand about 10 million annually in 2008 and 2009 to maintain public services <\s>
<s> new zealand's support amounts to 80 of tokelau's recurrent government budget <\s>
<s> an international trust fund currently worth nearly us 32 million was established in 2004 to provide tokelau an independent source of revenue <\s>
<s> the principal sources of revenue come from sales of copra postage stamps souvenir coins and handicrafts <\s>
<s> despite strong finances and underlying fundamentals the swedish economy slid into recession in the third quarter of 2008 and growth continued downward in 2009 as deteriorating global conditions reduced export demand and consumption <\s>
<s> strong exports of commodities and a return to profitability by sweden's banking sector drove the strong rebound in 2010 <\s>
<s> switzerland switzerland is a peaceful prosperous and modern market economy with low unemployment a highly skilled labor force and a per capita gdp among the highest in the world <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy benefits from a highly developed service sector led by financial services and a manufacturing industry that specializes in high-technology knowledge-based production <\s>
<s> the swiss have brought their economic practices largely into conformity with the eu's in order to enhance their international competitiveness but some trade protectionism remains particularly for its small agricultural sector <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis and resulting economic downturn put switzerland in a recession in 2009 as global export demand stalled <\s>
<s> the swiss national bank during this period effectively implemented a zero-interest rate policy in a bid to boost the economy and prevent appreciation of the franc <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy grew 2.8 in 2010 when bern implemented a third fiscal stimulus program but its prized banking sector has recently faced significant challenges <\s>
<s> the country's largest banks suffered sizable losses in 2008-09 leading its largest bank to accept a government rescue deal in late 2008 <\s>
<s> switzerland has also come under increasing pressure from individual neighboring countries the eu the us and international institutions to reform its banking secrecy laws <\s>
<s> consequently the government agreed to conform to oecd regulations on administrative assistance in tax matters including tax evasion <\s>
<s> the government has renegotiated its double taxation agreements with numerous countries including the us to incorporate the oecd standard and it is working with germany and the uk to resolve outsanding issues particularly the possibility of imposing taxes on bank deposits held by foreigners <\s>
<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>
<s> syria syrian economic growth slowed to 1.8 in 2009 as the global economic crisis affected oil prices and the economies of syria's key export partners and sources of investment <\s>
<s> damascus has implemented modest economic reforms in the past few years including cutting lending interest rates opening private banks consolidating all of the multiple exchange rates raising prices on some subsidized items most notably gasoline and cement and establishing the damascus stock exchange which began operations in 2009 <\s>
<s> in addition president asad signed legislative decrees to encourage corporate ownership reform and to allow the central bank to issue treasury bills and bonds for government debt <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy remains highly controlled by the government <\s>
<s> long-run economic constraints include declining oil production high unemployment rising budget deficits and increasing pressure on water supplies caused by heavy use in agriculture rapid population growth industrial expansion and water pollution <\s>
<s> taiwan taiwan has a dynamic capitalist economy with gradually decreasing government guidance of investment and foreign trade <\s>
<s> in keeping with this trend some large state-owned banks and industrial firms have been privatized <\s>
<s> exports led by electronics and machinery generate about 70 of taiwan's gdp growth and have provided the primary impetus for economic development <\s>
<s> this heavy dependence on exports makes the economy vulnerable to downturns in world demand <\s>
<s> in 2009 taiwan's gdp fell by 1.9 due primarily to a 20 year-on-year decline in exports <\s>
<s> gdp grew more than 8 in 2010 as exports returned to the level of previous years <\s>
<s> taiwan's diplomatic isolation low birth rate and rapidly aging population are major long-term challenges <\s>
<s> free trade agreements have proliferated in east asia over the past several years but so far taiwan has been excluded from this greater economic integration largely for reasons of diplomacy <\s>
<s> taiwan's birth rate of only 1.2 child per woman is among the lowest in the world raising the prospect of future labor shortages falling domestic demand and declining tax revenues <\s>
<s> taiwan's population is aging quickly with the number of people over 65 accounting for 10.8 of the island's total population as of the end of 2009 <\s>
<s> the island runs a large trade surplus and its foreign reserves are the world's fourth largest behind china japan and russia <\s>
<s> since president ma ying-jeou took office in may 2008 cross-strait economic ties have increased significantly <\s>
<s> since 2005 china has overtaken the us to become taiwan's second-largest source of imports after japan <\s>
<s> china is also the island's number one destination for foreign direct investment <\s>
<s> taipei has focused much of its economic recovery effort on improving cross-strait economic integration <\s>
<s> three financial memorandums of understanding covering banking securities and insurance took effect in mid-january 2010 opening the island to greater investments from the mainland's financial firms and institutional investors and providing new opportunities for taiwan financial firms to operate in china <\s>
<s> taiwan and the mainland in june 2010 signed the landmark economic cooperation framework agreement ecfa an agreement similar to a free-trade agreement deal that will increase cross-strait economic ties by lowering tariffs on a number of goods <\s>
<s> taiwan's goverment has said that the ecfa will serve as a stepping stone toward trade pacts with other regional partners and announced the beginning of negotiations on such an agreement with singapore in august <\s>
<s> tajikistan tajikistan has one of the lowest per capita gdps among the 15 former soviet republics <\s>
<s> because of a lack of employment opportunities in tajikistan nearly half of the labor force works abroad primarily in russia and kazakhstan supporting families in tajikistan through remittances <\s>
<s> the exact number of labor migrants is unknown but estimated at around 1 million <\s>
<s> less than 7 of the land area is arable <\s>
<s> cotton is the most important crop but this sector is burdened with debt and obsolete infrastructure moreover government has encouraged a gradual transition away from cotton and towards food cultivation due to its concerns about feeding the population <\s>
<s> mineral resources include silver gold uranium and tungsten <\s>
<s> industry consists only of a large aluminum plant hydropower facilities and small obsolete factories mostly in light industry and food processing <\s>
<s> the civil war 1992-97 severely damaged the already weak economic infrastructure and caused a sharp decline in industrial and agricultural production <\s>
<s> tajikistan's economic situation remains fragile due to uneven implementation of structural reforms corruption weak governance seasonal power shortages and the external debt burden <\s>
<s> a debt restructuring agreement was reached with russia in december 2002 including a 250 million write-off of tajikistan's 300 million debt <\s>
<s> completion of the sangtuda i hydropower dam finished in 2009 with russian investment and the sangtuda ii and rogun dams will add substantially to electricity output <\s>
<s> if finished according to tajik plans rogun will be the world's tallest dam <\s>
<s> the world bank in 2010 agreed to fund safety and feasibility studies for the rogun dam <\s>
<s> favorable reports from these studies could increase investor interest in the project which has been stalled due to lack of funding <\s>
<s> tajikistan has also received substantial infrastructure development loans from the chinese government to improve roads and an electricity transmission network <\s>
<s> to help increase north-south trade the us funded a 36 million bridge which opened in august 2007 and links tajikistan and afghanistan <\s>
<s> while tajikistan has experienced steady economic growth since 1997 more than half of the population continues to live in poverty <\s>
<s> economic growth reached 10.6 in 2004 but dropped below 8 in 2005-08 as the effects of higher oil prices and then the international financial crisis began to register mainly in the form of lower prices for key export commodities and lower remittances from tajiks working abroad due to the global economic downturn <\s>
<s> in 2009 gdp growth dropped to 3.4 as a result of the world recession <\s>
<s> tanzania tanzania is one of the world's poorest economies in terms of per capita income however tanzania average 7 gdp growth per year between 2000 and 2008 on strong gold production and tourism <\s>
<s> the economy depends heavily on agriculture which accounts for more than one-fourth of gdp provides 85 of exports and employs about 60 of the work force <\s>
<s> the world bank the imf and bilateral donors have provided funds to rehabilitate tanzania's aging economic infrastructure including rail and port infrastructure that are important trade links for inland countries <\s>
<s> recent banking reforms have helped increase private-sector growth and investment and the government has increased spending on agriculture to 7 of its budget <\s>
<s> continued donor assistance and solid macroeconomic policies supported a positive growth rate despite the world recession <\s>
<s> in 2008 tanzania received the world's largest millennium challenge compact grant worth 698 million <\s>
<s> dar es salaam used fiscal stimulus and loosened monitary policy to ease the impact of the global recession <\s>
<s> gdp growth in 2009-10 was a respectable 6 per year due to high gold prices and increased production <\s>
<s> thailand with a well-developed infrastructure a free-enterprise economy generally pro-investment policies and strong export industries thailand enjoyed solid growth from 2000 to 2008 averaging more than 4 per year as it recovered from the asian financial crisis of 1997-98 <\s>
<s> thai exports mostly machinery and electronic components agricultural commodities and jewelry continue to drive the economy accounting for more than half of gdp <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis of 2008-09 severely cut thailand's exports with most sectors experiencing double-digit drops <\s>
<s> in 2009 the economy contracted 2.2 <\s>
<s> in 2010 thailand's economy expanded 7.6 its fastest pace since 1995 as exports rebounded from their depressed 2009 level <\s>
<s> antigovernment protests during march-may and the country's polarized political situation had at most a temporary impact on business and consumer confidence <\s>
<s> although tourism was hit hard during the protests its quick recovery helped boost consumer confidence to new highs <\s>
<s> moreover business and investor sentiment remained buoyant as thailand's stock market grew almost 5 during the three-month period <\s>
<s> the economy probably will continue to experience high grow well into 2011 <\s>
<s> timor-leste in late 1999 about 70 of the economic infrastructure of timor-leste was laid waste by indonesian troops and anti-independence militias <\s>
<s> three hundred thousand people fled westward <\s>
<s> over the next three years a massive international program manned by 5,000 peacekeepers (8 000 at peak and 1,300 police officers led to substantial reconstruction in both urban and rural areas <\s>
<s> by the end of 2005 refugees had returned or had settled in indonesia <\s>

<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>
<s> syria syrian economic growth slowed to 1.8 in 2009 as the global economic crisis affected oil prices and the economies of syria's key export partners and sources of investment <\s>
<s> damascus has implemented modest economic reforms in the past few years including cutting lending interest rates opening private banks consolidating all of the multiple exchange rates raising prices on some subsidized items most notably gasoline and cement and establishing the damascus stock exchange which began operations in 2009 <\s>
<s> in addition president asad signed legislative decrees to encourage corporate ownership reform and to allow the central bank to issue treasury bills and bonds for government debt <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy remains highly controlled by the government <\s>
<s> long-run economic constraints include declining oil production high unemployment rising budget deficits and increasing pressure on water supplies caused by heavy use in agriculture rapid population growth industrial expansion and water pollution <\s>
<s> taiwan taiwan has a dynamic capitalist economy with gradually decreasing government guidance of investment and foreign trade <\s>
<s> in keeping with this trend some large state-owned banks and industrial firms have been privatized <\s>
<s> exports led by electronics and machinery generate about 70 of taiwan's gdp growth and have provided the primary impetus for economic development <\s>
<s> this heavy dependence on exports makes the economy vulnerable to downturns in world demand <\s>
<s> in 2009 taiwan's gdp fell by 1.9 due primarily to a 20 year-on-year decline in exports <\s>
<s> gdp grew more than 8 in 2010 as exports returned to the level of previous years <\s>
<s> taiwan's diplomatic isolation low birth rate and rapidly aging population are major long-term challenges <\s>
<s> free trade agreements have proliferated in east asia over the past several years but so far taiwan has been excluded from this greater economic integration largely for reasons of diplomacy <\s>
<s> taiwan's birth rate of only 1.2 child per woman is among the lowest in the world raising the prospect of future labor shortages falling domestic demand and declining tax revenues <\s>
<s> taiwan's population is aging quickly with the number of people over 65 accounting for 10.8 of the island's total population as of the end of 2009 <\s>
<s> the island runs a large trade surplus and its foreign reserves are the world's fourth largest behind china japan and russia <\s>
<s> since president ma ying-jeou took office in may 2008 cross-strait economic ties have increased significantly <\s>
<s> since 2005 china has overtaken the us to become taiwan's second-largest source of imports after japan <\s>
<s> china is also the island's number one destination for foreign direct investment <\s>
<s> taipei has focused much of its economic recovery effort on improving cross-strait economic integration <\s>
<s> three financial memorandums of understanding covering banking securities and insurance took effect in mid-january 2010 opening the island to greater investments from the mainland's financial firms and institutional investors and providing new opportunities for taiwan financial firms to operate in china <\s>
<s> taiwan and the mainland in june 2010 signed the landmark economic cooperation framework agreement ecfa an agreement similar to a free-trade agreement deal that will increase cross-strait economic ties by lowering tariffs on a number of goods <\s>
<s> taiwan's goverment has said that the ecfa will serve as a stepping stone toward trade pacts with other regional partners and announced the beginning of negotiations on such an agreement with singapore in august <\s>
<s> tajikistan tajikistan has one of the lowest per capita gdps among the 15 former soviet republics <\s>
<s> because of a lack of employment opportunities in tajikistan nearly half of the labor force works abroad primarily in russia and kazakhstan supporting families in tajikistan through remittances <\s>
<s> the exact number of labor migrants is unknown but estimated at around 1 million <\s>
<s> less than 7 of the land area is arable <\s>
<s> cotton is the most important crop but this sector is burdened with debt and obsolete infrastructure moreover government has encouraged a gradual transition away from cotton and towards food cultivation due to its concerns about feeding the population <\s>
<s> mineral resources include silver gold uranium and tungsten <\s>
<s> industry consists only of a large aluminum plant hydropower facilities and small obsolete factories mostly in light industry and food processing <\s>
<s> the civil war 1992-97 severely damaged the already weak economic infrastructure and caused a sharp decline in industrial and agricultural production <\s>
<s> tajikistan's economic situation remains fragile due to uneven implementation of structural reforms corruption weak governance seasonal power shortages and the external debt burden <\s>
<s> a debt restructuring agreement was reached with russia in december 2002 including a 250 million write-off of tajikistan's 300 million debt <\s>
<s> completion of the sangtuda i hydropower dam finished in 2009 with russian investment and the sangtuda ii and rogun dams will add substantially to electricity output <\s>
<s> if finished according to tajik plans rogun will be the world's tallest dam <\s>
<s> the world bank in 2010 agreed to fund safety and feasibility studies for the rogun dam <\s>
<s> favorable reports from these studies could increase investor interest in the project which has been stalled due to lack of funding <\s>
<s> tajikistan has also received substantial infrastructure development loans from the chinese government to improve roads and an electricity transmission network <\s>
<s> to help increase north-south trade the us funded a 36 million bridge which opened in august 2007 and links tajikistan and afghanistan <\s>
<s> while tajikistan has experienced steady economic growth since 1997 more than half of the population continues to live in poverty <\s>
<s> economic growth reached 10.6 in 2004 but dropped below 8 in 2005-08 as the effects of higher oil prices and then the international financial crisis began to register mainly in the form of lower prices for key export commodities and lower remittances from tajiks working abroad due to the global economic downturn <\s>
<s> in 2009 gdp growth dropped to 3.4 as a result of the world recession <\s>
<s> tanzania tanzania is one of the world's poorest economies in terms of per capita income however tanzania average 7 gdp growth per year between 2000 and 2008 on strong gold production and tourism <\s>
<s> the economy depends heavily on agriculture which accounts for more than one-fourth of gdp provides 85 of exports and employs about 60 of the work force <\s>
<s> the world bank the imf and bilateral donors have provided funds to rehabilitate tanzania's aging economic infrastructure including rail and port infrastructure that are important trade links for inland countries <\s>
<s> recent banking reforms have helped increase private-sector growth and investment and the government has increased spending on agriculture to 7 of its budget <\s>
<s> continued donor assistance and solid macroeconomic policies supported a positive growth rate despite the world recession <\s>
<s> in 2008 tanzania received the world's largest millennium challenge compact grant worth 698 million <\s>
<s> dar es salaam used fiscal stimulus and loosened monitary policy to ease the impact of the global recession <\s>
<s> gdp growth in 2009-10 was a respectable 6 per year due to high gold prices and increased production <\s>
<s> thailand with a well-developed infrastructure a free-enterprise economy generally pro-investment policies and strong export industries thailand enjoyed solid growth from 2000 to 2008 averaging more than 4 per year as it recovered from the asian financial crisis of 1997-98 <\s>
<s> thai exports mostly machinery and electronic components agricultural commodities and jewelry continue to drive the economy accounting for more than half of gdp <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis of 2008-09 severely cut thailand's exports with most sectors experiencing double-digit drops <\s>
<s> in 2009 the economy contracted 2.2 <\s>
<s> in 2010 thailand's economy expanded 7.6 its fastest pace since 1995 as exports rebounded from their depressed 2009 level <\s>
<s> antigovernment protests during march-may and the country's polarized political situation had at most a temporary impact on business and consumer confidence <\s>
<s> although tourism was hit hard during the protests its quick recovery helped boost consumer confidence to new highs <\s>
<s> moreover business and investor sentiment remained buoyant as thailand's stock market grew almost 5 during the three-month period <\s>
<s> the economy probably will continue to experience high grow well into 2011 <\s>
<s> timor-leste in late 1999 about 70 of the economic infrastructure of timor-leste was laid waste by indonesian troops and anti-independence militias <\s>
<s> three hundred thousand people fled westward <\s>
<s> over the next three years a massive international program manned by 5,000 peacekeepers (8 000 at peak and 1,300 police officers led to substantial reconstruction in both urban and rural areas <\s>
<s> by the end of 2005 refugees had returned or had settled in indonesia <\s>
<s> the country continues to face great challenges in rebuilding its infrastructure strengthening the civil administration and generating jobs for young people entering the work force <\s>
<s> the development of oil and gas resources in offshore waters has greatly supplemented government revenues <\s>
<s> this technology-intensive industry however has done little to create jobs for the unemployed because there are no production facilities in timor <\s>
<s> gas is piped to australia <\s>
<s> in june 2005 the national parliament unanimously approved the creation of a petroleum fund to serve as a repository for all petroleum revenues and to preserve the value of timor-leste's petroleum wealth for future generations <\s>
<s> the fund held assets of us 5.3 billion as of october 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy has been little impacted by the global financial crisis and continues to recover strongly from the mid 2006 outbreak of violence and civil unrest which disrupted both private and public sector economic activity <\s>
<s> the government in 2008 resettled tens of thousands of an estimated 100,000 internally displaced persons idps ); most idps returned home by early 2009 <\s>
<s> the underlying economic policy challenge the country faces remains how best to use oil-and-gas wealth to lift the non-oil economy onto a higher growth path and to reduce poverty <\s>
<s> togo this small sub-saharan economy suffers from anemic economic growth and depends heavily on both commercial and subsistence agriculture which provides employment for 65 of the labor force <\s>
<s> some basic foodstuffs must still be imported <\s>
<s> cocoa coffee and cotton generate about 40 of export earnings with cotton being the most important cash crop <\s>
<s> togo is the world's fourth-largest producer of phosphate <\s>
<s> the government's decade-long effort supported by the world bank and the imf to implement economic reform measures encourage foreign investment and bring revenues in line with expenditures has moved slowly <\s>
<s> progress depends on follow through on privatization increased openness in government financial operations progress toward legislative elections and continued support from foreign donors <\s>
<s> togo is on track with its imf extended credit facility and reached a hipc debt relief completion point in 2010 at which 95 of the country's debt was forgiven <\s>
<s> economic growth prospects remain marginal due to declining cotton production and underinvestment in phosphate mining <\s>
<s> tokelau tokelau's small size three villages isolation and lack of resources greatly restrain economic development and confine agriculture to the subsistence level <\s>
<s> the people rely heavily on aid from new zealand about 10 million annually in 2008 and 2009 to maintain public services <\s>
<s> new zealand's support amounts to 80 of tokelau's recurrent government budget <\s>
<s> an international trust fund currently worth nearly us 32 million was established in 2004 to provide tokelau an independent source of revenue <\s>
<s> the principal sources of revenue come from sales of copra postage stamps souvenir coins and handicrafts <\s>
<s> despite strong finances and underlying fundamentals the swedish economy slid into recession in the third quarter of 2008 and growth continued downward in 2009 as deteriorating global conditions reduced export demand and consumption <\s>
<s> strong exports of commodities and a return to profitability by sweden's banking sector drove the strong rebound in 2010 <\s>
<s> switzerland switzerland is a peaceful prosperous and modern market economy with low unemployment a highly skilled labor force and a per capita gdp among the highest in the world <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy benefits from a highly developed service sector led by financial services and a manufacturing industry that specializes in high-technology knowledge-based production <\s>
<s> the swiss have brought their economic practices largely into conformity with the eu's in order to enhance their international competitiveness but some trade protectionism remains particularly for its small agricultural sector <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis and resulting economic downturn put switzerland in a recession in 2009 as global export demand stalled <\s>
<s> the swiss national bank during this period effectively implemented a zero-interest rate policy in a bid to boost the economy and prevent appreciation of the franc <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy grew 2.8 in 2010 when bern implemented a third fiscal stimulus program but its prized banking sector has recently faced significant challenges <\s>
<s> the country's largest banks suffered sizable losses in 2008-09 leading its largest bank to accept a government rescue deal in late 2008 <\s>
<s> switzerland has also come under increasing pressure from individual neighboring countries the eu the us and international institutions to reform its banking secrecy laws <\s>
<s> consequently the government agreed to conform to oecd regulations on administrative assistance in tax matters including tax evasion <\s>
<s> the government has renegotiated its double taxation agreements with numerous countries including the us to incorporate the oecd standard and it is working with germany and the uk to resolve outsanding issues particularly the possibility of imposing taxes on bank deposits held by foreigners <\s>
<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>

<s> cotton is the most important crop but this sector is burdened with debt and obsolete infrastructure moreover government has encouraged a gradual transition away from cotton and towards food cultivation due to its concerns about feeding the population <\s>
<s> mineral resources include silver gold uranium and tungsten <\s>
<s> industry consists only of a large aluminum plant hydropower facilities and small obsolete factories mostly in light industry and food processing <\s>
<s> the civil war 1992-97 severely damaged the already weak economic infrastructure and caused a sharp decline in industrial and agricultural production <\s>
<s> tajikistan's economic situation remains fragile due to uneven implementation of structural reforms corruption weak governance seasonal power shortages and the external debt burden <\s>
<s> a debt restructuring agreement was reached with russia in december 2002 including a 250 million write-off of tajikistan's 300 million debt <\s>
<s> completion of the sangtuda i hydropower dam finished in 2009 with russian investment and the sangtuda ii and rogun dams will add substantially to electricity output <\s>
<s> if finished according to tajik plans rogun will be the world's tallest dam <\s>
<s> the world bank in 2010 agreed to fund safety and feasibility studies for the rogun dam <\s>
<s> favorable reports from these studies could increase investor interest in the project which has been stalled due to lack of funding <\s>
<s> tajikistan has also received substantial infrastructure development loans from the chinese government to improve roads and an electricity transmission network <\s>
<s> to help increase north-south trade the us funded a 36 million bridge which opened in august 2007 and links tajikistan and afghanistan <\s>
<s> while tajikistan has experienced steady economic growth since 1997 more than half of the population continues to live in poverty <\s>
<s> economic growth reached 10.6 in 2004 but dropped below 8 in 2005-08 as the effects of higher oil prices and then the international financial crisis began to register mainly in the form of lower prices for key export commodities and lower remittances from tajiks working abroad due to the global economic downturn <\s>
<s> in 2009 gdp growth dropped to 3.4 as a result of the world recession <\s>
<s> tanzania tanzania is one of the world's poorest economies in terms of per capita income however tanzania average 7 gdp growth per year between 2000 and 2008 on strong gold production and tourism <\s>
<s> the economy depends heavily on agriculture which accounts for more than one-fourth of gdp provides 85 of exports and employs about 60 of the work force <\s>
<s> the world bank the imf and bilateral donors have provided funds to rehabilitate tanzania's aging economic infrastructure including rail and port infrastructure that are important trade links for inland countries <\s>
<s> recent banking reforms have helped increase private-sector growth and investment and the government has increased spending on agriculture to 7 of its budget <\s>
<s> continued donor assistance and solid macroeconomic policies supported a positive growth rate despite the world recession <\s>
<s> in 2008 tanzania received the world's largest millennium challenge compact grant worth 698 million <\s>
<s> dar es salaam used fiscal stimulus and loosened monitary policy to ease the impact of the global recession <\s>
<s> gdp growth in 2009-10 was a respectable 6 per year due to high gold prices and increased production <\s>
<s> thailand with a well-developed infrastructure a free-enterprise economy generally pro-investment policies and strong export industries thailand enjoyed solid growth from 2000 to 2008 averaging more than 4 per year as it recovered from the asian financial crisis of 1997-98 <\s>
<s> thai exports mostly machinery and electronic components agricultural commodities and jewelry continue to drive the economy accounting for more than half of gdp <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis of 2008-09 severely cut thailand's exports with most sectors experiencing double-digit drops <\s>
<s> in 2009 the economy contracted 2.2 <\s>
<s> in 2010 thailand's economy expanded 7.6 its fastest pace since 1995 as exports rebounded from their depressed 2009 level <\s>
<s> antigovernment protests during march-may and the country's polarized political situation had at most a temporary impact on business and consumer confidence <\s>
<s> although tourism was hit hard during the protests its quick recovery helped boost consumer confidence to new highs <\s>
<s> moreover business and investor sentiment remained buoyant as thailand's stock market grew almost 5 during the three-month period <\s>
<s> the economy probably will continue to experience high grow well into 2011 <\s>
<s> timor-leste in late 1999 about 70 of the economic infrastructure of timor-leste was laid waste by indonesian troops and anti-independence militias <\s>
<s> three hundred thousand people fled westward <\s>
<s> over the next three years a massive international program manned by 5,000 peacekeepers (8 000 at peak and 1,300 police officers led to substantial reconstruction in both urban and rural areas <\s>
<s> by the end of 2005 refugees had returned or had settled in indonesia <\s>
<s> the country continues to face great challenges in rebuilding its infrastructure strengthening the civil administration and generating jobs for young people entering the work force <\s>
<s> the development of oil and gas resources in offshore waters has greatly supplemented government revenues <\s>
<s> this technology-intensive industry however has done little to create jobs for the unemployed because there are no production facilities in timor <\s>
<s> gas is piped to australia <\s>
<s> in june 2005 the national parliament unanimously approved the creation of a petroleum fund to serve as a repository for all petroleum revenues and to preserve the value of timor-leste's petroleum wealth for future generations <\s>
<s> the fund held assets of us 5.3 billion as of october 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy has been little impacted by the global financial crisis and continues to recover strongly from the mid 2006 outbreak of violence and civil unrest which disrupted both private and public sector economic activity <\s>
<s> the government in 2008 resettled tens of thousands of an estimated 100,000 internally displaced persons idps ); most idps returned home by early 2009 <\s>
<s> the underlying economic policy challenge the country faces remains how best to use oil-and-gas wealth to lift the non-oil economy onto a higher growth path and to reduce poverty <\s>
<s> togo this small sub-saharan economy suffers from anemic economic growth and depends heavily on both commercial and subsistence agriculture which provides employment for 65 of the labor force <\s>
<s> some basic foodstuffs must still be imported <\s>
<s> cocoa coffee and cotton generate about 40 of export earnings with cotton being the most important cash crop <\s>
<s> togo is the world's fourth-largest producer of phosphate <\s>
<s> the government's decade-long effort supported by the world bank and the imf to implement economic reform measures encourage foreign investment and bring revenues in line with expenditures has moved slowly <\s>
<s> progress depends on follow through on privatization increased openness in government financial operations progress toward legislative elections and continued support from foreign donors <\s>
<s> togo is on track with its imf extended credit facility and reached a hipc debt relief completion point in 2010 at which 95 of the country's debt was forgiven <\s>
<s> economic growth prospects remain marginal due to declining cotton production and underinvestment in phosphate mining <\s>
<s> tokelau tokelau's small size three villages isolation and lack of resources greatly restrain economic development and confine agriculture to the subsistence level <\s>
<s> the people rely heavily on aid from new zealand about 10 million annually in 2008 and 2009 to maintain public services <\s>
<s> new zealand's support amounts to 80 of tokelau's recurrent government budget <\s>
<s> an international trust fund currently worth nearly us 32 million was established in 2004 to provide tokelau an independent source of revenue <\s>
<s> the principal sources of revenue come from sales of copra postage stamps souvenir coins and handicrafts <\s>
<s> despite strong finances and underlying fundamentals the swedish economy slid into recession in the third quarter of 2008 and growth continued downward in 2009 as deteriorating global conditions reduced export demand and consumption <\s>
<s> strong exports of commodities and a return to profitability by sweden's banking sector drove the strong rebound in 2010 <\s>
<s> switzerland switzerland is a peaceful prosperous and modern market economy with low unemployment a highly skilled labor force and a per capita gdp among the highest in the world <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy benefits from a highly developed service sector led by financial services and a manufacturing industry that specializes in high-technology knowledge-based production <\s>
<s> the swiss have brought their economic practices largely into conformity with the eu's in order to enhance their international competitiveness but some trade protectionism remains particularly for its small agricultural sector <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis and resulting economic downturn put switzerland in a recession in 2009 as global export demand stalled <\s>
<s> the swiss national bank during this period effectively implemented a zero-interest rate policy in a bid to boost the economy and prevent appreciation of the franc <\s>
<s> switzerland's economy grew 2.8 in 2010 when bern implemented a third fiscal stimulus program but its prized banking sector has recently faced significant challenges <\s>
<s> the country's largest banks suffered sizable losses in 2008-09 leading its largest bank to accept a government rescue deal in late 2008 <\s>
<s> switzerland has also come under increasing pressure from individual neighboring countries the eu the us and international institutions to reform its banking secrecy laws <\s>
<s> consequently the government agreed to conform to oecd regulations on administrative assistance in tax matters including tax evasion <\s>
<s> the government has renegotiated its double taxation agreements with numerous countries including the us to incorporate the oecd standard and it is working with germany and the uk to resolve outsanding issues particularly the possibility of imposing taxes on bank deposits held by foreigners <\s>
<s> parliament passed the first five double-taxation agreements including that with the us in march 2010 but the agreements are subject to public referendum <\s>
<s> in 2009 swiss financial regulators ordered the country's largest bank to reveal at washington's behest the names of us account-holders suspected of using the bank to commit tax fraud <\s>
<s> these steps will have a lasting impact on switzerland's long history of bank secrecy <\s>
<s> syria syrian economic growth slowed to 1.8 in 2009 as the global economic crisis affected oil prices and the economies of syria's key export partners and sources of investment <\s>
<s> damascus has implemented modest economic reforms in the past few years including cutting lending interest rates opening private banks consolidating all of the multiple exchange rates raising prices on some subsidized items most notably gasoline and cement and establishing the damascus stock exchange which began operations in 2009 <\s>
<s> in addition president asad signed legislative decrees to encourage corporate ownership reform and to allow the central bank to issue treasury bills and bonds for government debt <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy remains highly controlled by the government <\s>
<s> long-run economic constraints include declining oil production high unemployment rising budget deficits and increasing pressure on water supplies caused by heavy use in agriculture rapid population growth industrial expansion and water pollution <\s>
<s> taiwan taiwan has a dynamic capitalist economy with gradually decreasing government guidance of investment and foreign trade <\s>
<s> in keeping with this trend some large state-owned banks and industrial firms have been privatized <\s>
<s> exports led by electronics and machinery generate about 70 of taiwan's gdp growth and have provided the primary impetus for economic development <\s>
<s> this heavy dependence on exports makes the economy vulnerable to downturns in world demand <\s>
<s> in 2009 taiwan's gdp fell by 1.9 due primarily to a 20 year-on-year decline in exports <\s>
<s> gdp grew more than 8 in 2010 as exports returned to the level of previous years <\s>
<s> taiwan's diplomatic isolation low birth rate and rapidly aging population are major long-term challenges <\s>
<s> free trade agreements have proliferated in east asia over the past several years but so far taiwan has been excluded from this greater economic integration largely for reasons of diplomacy <\s>
<s> taiwan's birth rate of only 1.2 child per woman is among the lowest in the world raising the prospect of future labor shortages falling domestic demand and declining tax revenues <\s>
<s> taiwan's population is aging quickly with the number of people over 65 accounting for 10.8 of the island's total population as of the end of 2009 <\s>
<s> the island runs a large trade surplus and its foreign reserves are the world's fourth largest behind china japan and russia <\s>
<s> since president ma ying-jeou took office in may 2008 cross-strait economic ties have increased significantly <\s>
<s> since 2005 china has overtaken the us to become taiwan's second-largest source of imports after japan <\s>
<s> china is also the island's number one destination for foreign direct investment <\s>
<s> taipei has focused much of its economic recovery effort on improving cross-strait economic integration <\s>
<s> three financial memorandums of understanding covering banking securities and insurance took effect in mid-january 2010 opening the island to greater investments from the mainland's financial firms and institutional investors and providing new opportunities for taiwan financial firms to operate in china <\s>
<s> taiwan and the mainland in june 2010 signed the landmark economic cooperation framework agreement ecfa an agreement similar to a free-trade agreement deal that will increase cross-strait economic ties by lowering tariffs on a number of goods <\s>
<s> taiwan's goverment has said that the ecfa will serve as a stepping stone toward trade pacts with other regional partners and announced the beginning of negotiations on such an agreement with singapore in august <\s>
<s> tajikistan tajikistan has one of the lowest per capita gdps among the 15 former soviet republics <\s>
<s> because of a lack of employment opportunities in tajikistan nearly half of the labor force works abroad primarily in russia and kazakhstan supporting families in tajikistan through remittances <\s>
<s> the exact number of labor migrants is unknown but estimated at around 1 million <\s>
